.2121		09 80		ora #$80			ora #kernel.args.timer.QUERY		; and query what frame we're on
.2123		85 f3		sta $f3				sta kernel.args.timer.units			; store in units parameter
.2125		20 f0 ff	jsr $fff0			jsr kernel.Clock.SetTimer			; jsr to Kernel Routine
.2128		b0 04		bcs $212e			bcs skipSet							; If Carry set, ignore
.212a		69 01		adc #$01			adc #$01							; if not add 1 to Accumulator for next frame
.212c		85 d0		sta $d0				sta $d0
.212e						skipSet:
.212e		20 64 21	jsr $2164			jsr SetTimer						; Let's get the kernel set up for the timer
.2131						loop:
.2131		20 37 21	jsr $2137			jsr handle_events					; This is my game loop
.2134		4c 31 21	jmp $2131			jmp loop
.2137						handle_events:
.2137		a5 f2		lda $f2				lda kernel.args.events.pending		; Peek at the queue to see if anything is pending
.2139		10 0b		bpl $2146			bpl done_handle_events				; Nothing to do
.213b		20 00 ff	jsr $ff00			jsr kernel.NextEvent				; Get the next event.
.213e		b0 06		bcs $2146			bcs done_handle_events				; If Carry is set, skip the handler
.2140		20 47 21	jsr $2147			jsr dispatch						; Handle the event
.2143		4c 37 21	jmp $2137			jmp handle_events					; go and check for another event
.2146						done_handle_events:

.2147						dispatch:
.2147		a5 a0		lda $a0				lda event.type						; get the event type from Kernel
.2149		c9 52		cmp #$52			cmp #kernel.event.timer.EXPIRED		; is the event timer.EXPIRED?

.214f		f0 11		beq $2162	        beq keypress

.2176						csLoop:

.2178		85 01		sta $01				sta MMU_IO_CTRL

.217c		9d 00 c0	sta $c000,x			sta $c000+$000,x 					; and save every 240 memory locations
.217f		9d f0 c0	sta $c0f0,x			sta $c000+$0f0,x 					;
.2182		9d e0 c1	sta $c1e0,x			sta $c000+$1e0,x 					; We're only going to loop once instead of
.2185		9d d0 c2	sta $c2d0,x			sta $c000+$2d0,x 					; nesting loops
.2188		9d c0 c3	sta $c3c0,x			sta $c000+$3c0,x

.2191		9d 00 c0	sta $c000,x			sta $c000+$000,x 					; do the same save groups
.2194		9d f0 c0	sta $c0f0,x			sta $c000+$0f0,x
